kha padmas brgyan pa'o / /
rim pa gsum pa'i lha snam la shar sgo'i g.yon du kun du bzang po sngon po sngo dmar dkar ba'i zhal gsum phyag drug gi g.yas rdo rje gri gug dgra sta /
g.yon dril bu thod pa tshangs mgo 'dzin pa la chos dbyings rdo rje mas 'khyud pa /
shar sgo'i g.yas su nam mkha'i snying po don grub lta bu la dri rdo rje mas 'khyud pa /
lho sgo'i g.yon du phyag na rdo rje ljang khu ljang dmar dkar ba'i zhal gsum phyag drug gi g.yas rdo rje gri gug dgra sta /
g.yon dril bu thod pa tshangs mgo 'dzin pa la sgra rdo rje mas 'khyud pa /
lho sgo'i g.yas su sa'i snying po rin 'byung lta bu la gzugs rdo rje mas 'khyud pa /
nub sgo'i g.yon du chos dbyings rdo rje ma phyag rdor lta bu la kun du bzang pos 'khyud pa /
nub sgo'i g.yas su sgrib pa rnam sel rnam snang lta bu la reg bya rdo rje mas 'khyud pa /
byang sgo'i g.yon du sgra rdo rje ma kun bzang lta bu la phyag rdor gyis 'khyud pa /
byang sgo'i g.yas su 'jig rten dbang phyug snang ba mtha' yas lta bu la ro rdo rje mas 'khyud pa /
thams cad kyang padma dkar po dang nyi ma'i gdan la rdo rje'i skyil dkrung gis bzhugs pa la yum rnams padma'i 'dug stang gis 'khyud pa'o / /
mer reg bya rdo rje ma sgrol ma lta bu la sgrib pa rnam sel gyis 'khyud pa /
bden bral du ro rdo rje ma gos dkar mo lta bu la 'jig rten dbang phyug gis 'khyud pa /
rlung du dri rdo rje ma spyan ma lta bu la nam mkha'i snying pos 'khyud pa /
dbang ldan du gzugs rdo rje ma mA ma ki lta bu la sa'i snying pos 'khyud pa /
thams cad kyang padma dmar po dang zla ba'i gdan la padma'i 'dug stang gis bzhugs pa la yab rnams rdo rje'i gdan gyis 'khyud pa'o / /
shar sgor khro bo shin du stobs don grub lta bu la rengs byed ma spyan ma lta bus 'khyud pa /
lho sgor khro bo rmongs byed rin 'byung lta bu la nga rgyal byed ma mA ma ki lta bus 'khyud pa /
nub sgor khro bo rengs byed rnam snang lta bu la shin du stobs ma sgrol ma lta bus 'khyud pa /
byang sgor khro bo nga rgyal byed 'od dpag med lta bu la rmongs byed ma dkar mo lta bus 'khyud pa /
khro bo rnams g.yas brgyad dang khro mo rnams g.yon brkyang gis gnas shing /
lha pho rnams gdan padma dkar po dang /
nyi ma /

nang gi shar dkar lho sngo nub dmar byang ljang dbus ser ba'i dbus su 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad pa ser po rdo rje'i phreng ba sngon pos bskor ba'i lte bar sna tshogs padma la gnas pa'i seng ge'i khri'i steng du sna tshogs padma dang zla ba /
